Compute Services

AWS Compute Services provide scalable, secure, and reliable virtual computing resources for your Django applications. This section covers deploying and managing your anihpj job posting platform on AWS infrastructure.

Amazon EC2 (Elastic Compute Cloud)

Category: Compute  |  Use Case: Web Application Hosting  |  Pricing: On-Demand, Reserved, Spot Instances  |  Last Updated: November 2025  |  Documentation: AWS EC2 Docs

Secure and resizable compute capacity in the cloud for hosting Django applications with automatic scaling, load balancing, and high availability.

рҹ“Ӣ Overview & Introduction

Amazon Elastic Compute Cloud (EC2) is a web service that provides secure, resizable compute capacity in the cloud. It's designed to make web-scale cloud computing easier for developers by providing complete control over computing resources.

рҹҺҜ Key Benefits
  • Elastic Computing: Scale capacity up or down within minutes
  • Complete Control: Root access to instances and full control over computing resources
  • Flexible Pricing: Pay only for what you use with multiple pricing models
  • Integrated: Seamlessly works with other AWS services
  • Secure: Built-in firewall, VPC, and IAM integration
  • Reliable: 99.99% SLA with multiple availability zones
рҹ’Ў When to Use EC2: Perfect for your anihpj Django job portal when you need full control over the server environment, custom configurations, or need to run background tasks, scheduled jobs, or WebSocket connections alongside your web application.
вҡ–пёҸ EC2 vs. Other Compute Services
EC2: Full control, persistent, traditional apps
Lambda: Serverless, event-driven, short tasks
ECS/EKS: Container orchestration
Elastic Beanstalk: Managed platform for web apps
Lightsail: Simplified VPS for simple apps
Fargate: Serverless containers
рҹҸ—пёҸ EC2 in AWS Ecosystem - Architecture Overview

в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  IAM (Identity & Access Management)                        в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  - EC2 instance roles and permissions                      в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ   в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

рҹ”§ Core Concepts

рҹ–ҘпёҸ EC2 Instances

An EC2 instance is a virtual server in Amazon's cloud. Think of it as a computer that you can configure and control, running your anihpj Django application.

рҹ“Ҡ Instance Lifecycle States
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ Pending в”Ӯ  вҶҗ Launch initiated, instance is being prepared
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
     в”Ӯ
     в–ј
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ Running в”Ӯ  вҶҗ Instance is running and you can connect to it
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ     Your Django app is serving traffic here!
     в”Ӯ
     в”ңв”Җв”ҖвҶ’ [Reboot] в”Җв”ҖвҶ’ Returns to Running
     в”Ӯ
     в–ј
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ Stopping в”Ӯ  вҶҗ Stop command issued, instance is shutting down
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
     в”Ӯ
     в–ј
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ Stopped в”Ӯ  вҶҗ Instance is stopped (not charged for compute)
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ     Still charged for EBS storage
     в”Ӯ
     в”ңв”Җв”ҖвҶ’ [Start] в”Җв”ҖвҶ’ Returns to Pending вҶ’ Running
     в”Ӯ
     в–ј
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ Terminating в”Ӯ  вҶҗ Delete command issued
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
       в”Ӯ
       в–ј
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ Terminated в”Ӯ  вҶҗ Instance deleted permanently (can't recover)
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
рҹҸ·пёҸ Instance Types

EC2 offers different instance types optimized for various use cases. For your Django job portal, you'll typically use General Purpose instances.

рҹ“Ӣ Instance Type Families
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ                    INSTANCE TYPE FAMILIES                         в”Ӯ
в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
в”Ӯ                                                                   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  T Family (Burstable Performance)                                в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ t3.micro, t3.small, t3.medium                                в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ рҹ’Ў Best for: Development, testing, low-traffic websites      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     вң… Perfect for: Starting your anihpj portal                   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  M Family (General Purpose - Balanced)                           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ m5.large, m5.xlarge, m5.2xlarge                              в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ рҹ’Ў Best for: Production web apps, small-to-medium databases  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     вң… Ideal for: Production anihpj with moderate traffic         в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  C Family (Compute Optimized)                                    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ c5.large, c5.xlarge, c5.2xlarge                              в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ рҹ’Ў Best for: CPU-intensive tasks, batch processing           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     вң… Use for: Heavy background job processing                   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  R Family (Memory Optimized)                                     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ r5.large, r5.xlarge, r5.2xlarge                              в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ рҹ’Ў Best for: In-memory caching, large datasets               в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     вң… Use for: Redis/Memcached for Django sessions               в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  I Family (Storage Optimized)                                    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ i3.large, i3.xlarge, i3.2xlarge                              в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ рҹ’Ў Best for: High I/O databases, data warehousing            в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  P/G Family (Accelerated Computing - GPU)                        в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ p3.2xlarge, g4dn.xlarge                                      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ рҹ’Ў Best for: Machine learning, video rendering               в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                   в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
рҹ”Қ Instance Naming Convention Explained
Example: m5.xlarge

в”Ңв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯmв”Ӯ5 в”Ӯxlargeв”Ӯ
в””в”¬в”ҳв””в”¬в”ҳв””в”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
 в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ   в””в”ҖвҶ’ Size: nano, micro, small, medium, large, xlarge, 2xlarge, etc.
 в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ       вҖў xlarge = 4 vCPUs, 16 GiB RAM (for m5 family)
 в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ       вҖў 2xlarge = 8 vCPUs, 32 GiB RAM
 в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ
 в”Ӯ  в””в”ҖвҶ’ Generation: 5 (latest generation for m family)
 в”Ӯ       вҖў Higher generation = better performance & newer features
 в”Ӯ       вҖў Always prefer latest generation when available
 в”Ӯ
 в””в”ҖвҶ’ Family: m (General Purpose, balanced compute/memory)
      вҖў t = Burstable
      вҖў m = General Purpose
      вҖў c = Compute Optimized
      вҖў r = Memory Optimized
      вҖў i = Storage Optimized

For anihpj Django Portal:
вҖў Development: t3.micro (1 vCPU, 1 GiB RAM) вҶ’ $0.0104/hour
вҖў Staging: t3.small (2 vCPUs, 2 GiB RAM) вҶ’ $0.0208/hour  
вҖў Production: m5.large (2 vCPUs, 8 GiB RAM) вҶ’ $0.096/hour
рҹ“Ҡ Instance Type Comparison for Django Job Portal
Instance Type vCPUs Memory (GiB) Network Price/Hour Best For
t3.micro 2 1 Up to 5 Gbps $0.0104 Development, testing
t3.small 2 2 Up to 5 Gbps $0.0208 Small production sites
t3.medium 2 4 Up to 5 Gbps $0.0416 Medium traffic jobpost
m5.large 2 8 Up to 10 Gbps $0.096 вӯҗ Recommended for production
m5.xlarge 4 16 Up to 10 Gbps $0.192 High traffic, heavy load
c5.large 2 4 Up to 10 Gbps $0.085 Compute-intensive tasks
рҹ’ҝ AMIs (Amazon Machine Images)

An AMI is a template that contains the software configuration (operating system, application server, and applications) required to launch your instance.

рҹ–јпёҸ AMI Types & Selection Process
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ                     AMI TYPES FOR DJANGO                      в”Ӯ
в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
в”Ӯ                                                               в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  1. AWS-Provided AMIs (Recommended)                          в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Amazon Linux 2023 (Latest)                            в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     в”Ӯ  вҖў Optimized for AWS, free tier eligible               в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     в”Ӯ  вҖў Includes AWS CLI and tools                          в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     в”Ӯ  вҖў вң… Great for production anihpj                       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     в”Ӯ                                                         в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Ubuntu Server 22.04 LTS                               в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     в”Ӯ  вҖў Popular for Django development                      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     в”Ӯ  вҖў Large community support                             в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     в”Ӯ  вҖў вң… Best for Django familiarity                       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     в”Ӯ                                                         в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     в””в”Җ Amazon Linux 2                                        в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ        вҖў Stable, long-term support                           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ        вҖў Good for enterprise applications                    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                               в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  2. Marketplace AMIs                                         в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Bitnami Django Stack                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     в”Ӯ  вҖў Pre-configured Django environment                   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     в”Ӯ  вҖў Includes PostgreSQL, Nginx, SSL                     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     в”Ӯ  вҖў вҡЎ Quick start for anihpj                            в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     в”Ӯ                                                         в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     в””в”Җ Various vendor solutions                              в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ        вҖў May have licensing costs                            в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                               в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  3. Community AMIs                                           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     в””в”Җ Shared by other AWS users                             в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ        вҖў Use with caution (verify source)                    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ        вҖў Free, but less support                              в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                               в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  4. Custom AMIs (Your Own)                                   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     в””в”Җ Create snapshot of configured anihpj instance         в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ        вҖў Pre-installed Django, dependencies                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ        вҖў Pre-configured settings                             в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ        вҖў вң… Perfect for scaling identical instances           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                               в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

рҹҢҚ Regions & Availability Zones

AWS infrastructure is distributed globally across Regions and Availability Zones for high availability and low latency.

рҹ—әпёҸ AWS Global Infrastructure for anihpj
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ                  AWS GLOBAL INFRASTRUCTURE                      в”Ӯ
в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
в”Ӯ                                                                 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  REGION: us-east-1 (N. Virginia) - Most services available     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Availability Zone A (use1-az1)                             в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Data Center 1, 2, 3                                     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ     вҖў anihpj-web-server-1 вҶҗ Place your Django app here      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ     вҖў Independent power, cooling, networking                в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ                                                              в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Availability Zone B (use1-az2)                             в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Data Center 4, 5, 6                                     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ     вҖў anihpj-web-server-2 вҶҗ Failover instance here          в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ     вҖў Physically separate from AZ-A                         в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ                                                              в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Availability Zone C (use1-az3)                             в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     в””в”Җ Data Center 7, 8, 9                                     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ        вҖў anihpj-web-server-3 вҶҗ Additional redundancy           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  REGION: eu-west-1 (Ireland) - European users                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Deploy here if serving European job seekers                в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     вҖў Lower latency for EU users                               в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ     вҖў GDPR compliance considerations                           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  REGION: ap-southeast-1 (Singapore) - Asian users              в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Deploy here for Asian market                               в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                 в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

Latency Considerations:
вҖў Same AZ: < 1ms
вҖў Different AZ (same region): 1-2ms
вҖў Different Region: 50-300ms (depends on distance)

For anihpj Job Portal:
вң… Multi-AZ Deployment: High availability within same region
вң… Multi-Region: Global reach for international job postings

рҹҡҖ Getting Started with EC2 for Django

рҹ“Ӣ Prerequisites
Before You Begin:
  • вң… AWS Account created (aws.amazon.com)
  • вң… IAM user with EC2 permissions (or use root account temporarily)
  • вң… AWS CLI installed (optional but recommended)
  • вң… SSH client installed (Linux/Mac: built-in, Windows: PuTTY or Windows Terminal)
  • вң… Your anihpj Django code ready in Git repository
рҹ”җ Required IAM Permissions
{
  "Version": "2012-10-17",
  "Statement": [
    {
      "Effect": "Allow",
      "Action": [
        "ec2:RunInstances",
        "ec2:TerminateInstances",
        "ec2:StopInstances",
        "ec2:StartInstances",
        "ec2:RebootInstances",
        "ec2:DescribeInstances",
        "ec2:DescribeImages",
        "ec2:DescribeKeyPairs",
        "ec2:DescribeSecurityGroups",
        "ec2:CreateKeyPair",
        "ec2:CreateSecurityGroup",
        "ec2:AuthorizeSecurityGroupIngress",
        "ec2:CreateTags",
        "ec2:DescribeVolumes",
        "ec2:AttachVolume"
      ],
      "Resource": "*"
    }
  ]
}

Save this as anihpj-ec2-policy.json and attach to your IAM user

рҹҺҜ Launch Your First EC2 Instance (Step-by-Step)
Step 1: Navigate to EC2 Console
1. Sign in to AWS Console (https://console.aws.amazon.com)
2. Search for "EC2" in the services search bar
3. Click "EC2" to open the EC2 Dashboard
4. Click orange "Launch Instance" button

рҹ“ё You should see:

Step 5: Configure Key Pair (Login Credentials)
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ

рҹ”Ң Connecting to Your EC2 Instance
Method 1: SSH Connection (Linux/Mac/Windows)
# 1. Set correct permissions on your key file
chmod 400 anihpj-keypair.pem

# 2. Get your instance public IP from EC2 console
# Example: 54.123.45.67

# 3. Connect using SSH
ssh -i "anihpj-keypair.pem" ubuntu@54.123.45.67

# First time connection will ask:
# "Are you sure you want to continue connecting (yes/no)?"
# Type: yes

# вң… You should now see:
# ubuntu@ip-172-31-10-10:~$
Welcome to Ubuntu 22.04.3 LTS (GNU/Linux 6.2.0-1009-aws x86_64) Last login: Mon Nov 3 10:30:15 2025 from 203.0.113.10 ubuntu@ip-172-31-10-10:~$
Method 2: EC2 Instance Connect (Browser-based)
1. Go to EC2 Console вҶ’ Instances
2. Select your instance (anihpj-django-production)
3. Click "Connect" button (top right)
4. Choose "EC2 Instance Connect" tab
5. Username: ubuntu
6. Click "Connect"

вң… Opens terminal in browser - no SSH client needed!

в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ  EC2 Instance Connect                       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ ubuntu@ip-172-31-10-10:~$            в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ                                       в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ                                       в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ  в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

рҹ’Ў Great for quick access without SSH keys!
Method 3: AWS Systems Manager Session Manager (Most Secure)
# No SSH keys needed, all access logged!

# 1. Install SSM agent (usually pre-installed on AWS AMIs)
# 2. Attach IAM role with SSM permissions to EC2 instance
# 3. Install AWS CLI locally
pip install awscli

# 4. Configure AWS CLI
aws configure

# 5. Start session
aws ssm start-session --target i-0abc123def456789

# вң… Secure connection without opening port 22!
# All commands logged to CloudWatch for audit
вң… Instance Running! Your EC2 instance is now ready. Next step: Deploy your anihpj Django application!

рҹ”‘ Key Features & Components

рҹ’ҫ Storage Options

EC2 provides multiple storage options for your Django application, each optimized for different use cases.

рҹ“Ҡ Storage Types Comparison
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ                     EC2 STORAGE OPTIONS                              в”Ӯ
в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
в”Ӯ                                                                      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  1. EBS (Elastic Block Store) - Persistent Network Storage          в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Type        в”Ӯ IOPS      в”Ӯ Throughput  в”Ӯ Use Case             в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ gp3 (SSD)    в”Ӯ 3K-16K    в”Ӯ 125-1000MB/sв”Ӯ вң… General Purpose   в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ              в”Ӯ           в”Ӯ             в”Ӯ    Boot volumes      в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ              в”Ӯ           в”Ӯ             в”Ӯ    Django app files  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ              в”Ӯ           в”Ӯ             в”Ӯ    Most cost-effect. в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ gp2 (SSD)    в”Ӯ 100-16K   в”Ӯ Varies      в”Ӯ Legacy, use gp3      в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ io2 (SSD)    в”Ӯ Up to 64K в”Ӯ Up to 1GB/s в”Ӯ High-performance DB  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ              в”Ӯ           в”Ӯ             в”Ӯ Mission-critical     в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ st1 (HDD)    в”Ӯ 500       в”Ӯ Up to 500MB в”Ӯ Big data, logs       в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ              в”Ӯ           в”Ӯ             в”Ӯ Sequential access    в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ sc1 (HDD)    в”Ӯ 250       в”Ӯ Up to 250MB в”Ӯ Cold storage         в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ              в”Ӯ           в”Ӯ             в”Ӯ Infrequent access    в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  EBS Features:                                                       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вң… Persistent (survives instance stop/start)                        в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вң… Snapshots for backup                                             в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вң… Encryption at rest                                               в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вң… Can attach/detach from instances                                 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вң… Replicated within AZ                                             в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  2. Instance Store - Ephemeral Local Storage                        в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Physically attached to host computer                        в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Very high IOPS (millions)                                   в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў вҡ пёҸ Data lost on instance stop/termination                    в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Use for: Temporary cache, buffers, scratch data            в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў вқҢ Don't use for: Django database, user uploads             в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  3. EFS (Elastic File System) - Shared Network File System          в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Shared across multiple EC2 instances                        в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Auto-scales (petabytes)                                     в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Use for: Shared media uploads in anihpj                     в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Multiple web servers accessing same files                   в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  4. S3 Integration - Object Storage                                 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Store Django static files (CSS, JS, images)                 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў User uploaded files (resumes, company logos)                в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Cheaper than EBS for large files                            в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Use django-storages library                                 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                      в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

For anihpj Job Portal:
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ  Component              в”Ӯ Storage Type            в”Ӯ
в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
в”Ӯ  OS & Django app        в”Ӯ EBS gp3 (20 GB)         в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  Database (if local)    в”Ӯ EBS gp3 (30 GB)         в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  Static files (prod)    в”Ӯ S3                      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  User uploads (resumes) в”Ӯ S3                      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  Application logs       в”Ӯ EBS + CloudWatch        в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  Session cache          в”Ӯ Redis on separate EBS   в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
рҹ’ҝ Attaching Additional EBS Volume
# Create new EBS volume for Django media files
aws ec2 create-volume \
    --volume-type gp3 \
    --size 30 \
    --availability-zone us-east-1a \
    --tag-specifications 'ResourceType=volume,Tags=[{Key=Name,Value=anihpj-media-storage}]'

# Output: vol-0abc123def456789

# Attach volume to instance
aws ec2 attach-volume \
    --volume-id vol-0abc123def456789 \
    --instance-id i-0abc123def456789 \
    --device /dev/sdf

# On the instance, format and mount
sudo mkfs -t ext4 /dev/xvdf
sudo mkdir /opt/anihpj/media
sudo mount /dev/xvdf /opt/anihpj/media

# Add to /etc/fstab for persistent mount
echo '/dev/xvdf /opt/anihpj/media ext4 defaults,nofail 0 2' | sudo tee -a /etc/fstab

# Update Django settings.py
# MEDIA_ROOT = '/opt/anihpj/media/'

Security Groups (Virtual Firewalls):
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ  anihpj-web-sg (Applied to Web Servers)                         в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ Inbound Rules:                                            в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў SSH (22) from 203.0.113.0/24 (your office)            в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў HTTP (80) from 0.0.0.0/0 (anywhere)                   в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў HTTPS (443) from 0.0.0.0/0 (anywhere)                 в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө  в”Ӯ

в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ  в”Ӯ

в”Ӯ  anihpj-db-sg (Applied to Database)                             в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ӯ

в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ    (security group reference - more secure)              в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө  в”Ӯ

в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў None needed (database doesn't initiate connections)   в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ  в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
рҹ”— Elastic IP Address (Static IP)
# Allocate Elastic IP
aws ec2 allocate-address --domain vpc

# Output:
# {
#     "PublicIp": "54.123.45.67",
#     "AllocationId": "eipalloc-0abc123",
#     "Domain": "vpc"
# }

# Associate with your instance
aws ec2 associate-address \
    --instance-id i-0abc123def456789 \
    --allocation-id eipalloc-0abc123

# Benefits for anihpj:
# вң… IP persists even if instance is stopped/started
# вң… Can quickly reassign to failover instance
# вң… Use in DNS records (A record for anihpj.com)
# вң… Simpler firewall rules
рҹ’Ў Elastic IP for Production: Always use Elastic IP for production Django apps so your DNS doesn't break when you restart instances. First 1 Elastic IP per running instance is free!
рҹҺҜ Placement Groups
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ                 PLACEMENT GROUP STRATEGIES                в”Ӯ
в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
в”Ӯ                                                           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  1. Cluster Placement Group                              в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Same Rack / Same AZ                                в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ                       в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ӮEC2 в”Ӯ в”ӮEC2 в”Ӯ в”ӮEC2 в”Ӯ в”ӮEC2 в”Ӯ                       в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ 1  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 2  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 3  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 4  в”Ӯ                       в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ                       в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… Low latency (microseconds)                       в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… High network throughput (10 Gbps)               в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вқҢ Single point of failure                         в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Use for: HPC, big data processing                 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  2. Spread Placement Group                               в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Different Racks / Multiple AZs                     в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Rack 1    Rack 2    Rack 3    Rack 4              в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ   в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ   в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ   в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ               в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ӮEC2 в”Ӯ   в”ӮEC2 в”Ӯ   в”ӮEC2 в”Ӯ   в”ӮEC2 в”Ӯ               в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ 1  в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ 2  в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ 3  в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ 4  в”Ӯ               в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ   в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ   в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ   в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ               в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… High availability                                в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… Fault tolerance                                  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… Max 7 instances per AZ                           в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Use for: Critical anihpj production servers       в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  3. Partition Placement Group                            в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Partitions with multiple instances                 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Part-1      Part-2      Part-3                     в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ   в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ   в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ                    в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ EC2  в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ EC2  в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ EC2  в”Ӯ                    в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ EC2  в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ EC2  в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ EC2  в”Ӯ                    в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ   в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ   в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ                    в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… Up to 7 partitions per AZ                        в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… Reduces correlated failures                      в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Use for: Distributed systems (Kafka, Hadoop)      в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ

рҹ”’ Security Features
рҹӣЎпёҸ Security Groups vs Network ACLs
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ         SECURITY GROUPS vs NETWORK ACLs                          в”Ӯ
в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  Security Groups (Instance-level Firewall)                      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў STATEFUL (return traffic auto-allowed)                  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Applied to ENI (Elastic Network Interface)              в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Only ALLOW rules (no deny)                              в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў All rules evaluated                                     в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ                                                             в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Example for anihpj-web-sg:                                в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ Inbound:                                             в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Rule 1: Allow SSH (22) from 203.0.113.0/24         в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Rule 2: Allow HTTP (80) from 0.0.0.0/0             в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Rule 3: Allow HTTPS (443) from 0.0.0.0/0           в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ                                                       в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ Outbound:                                            в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Rule 1: Allow all traffic to 0.0.0.0/0             в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  Network ACLs (Subnet-level Firewall)                           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў STATELESS (must allow return traffic explicitly)        в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Applied to entire subnet                                в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Both ALLOW and DENY rules                               в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Rules evaluated in order (lowest number first)          в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ                                                             в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Example for anihpj public subnet:                         в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ Inbound:                                             в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  100: Allow HTTP (80) from 0.0.0.0/0                 в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  110: Allow HTTPS (443) from 0.0.0.0/0               в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  120: Allow SSH (22) from 203.0.113.0/24             в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  130: Allow Ephemeral ports (1024-65535)             в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  *  : Deny all (implicit)                            в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ                                                       в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ Outbound:                                            в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  100: Allow HTTP (80) to 0.0.0.0/0                   в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  110: Allow HTTPS (443) to 0.0.0.0/0                 в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  120: Allow Ephemeral ports (1024-65535)             в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  *  : Deny all (implicit)                            в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ

в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Best Practice for anihpj:                                 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  1. Use Security Groups as primary defense                 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  2. Use Network ACLs for additional subnet-level rules     в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  3. Deny known malicious IPs at NACL level                 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
рҹ”‘ IAM Roles for EC2
// Create IAM role for anihpj EC2 instances
{
  "Version": "2012-10-17",
  "Statement": [
    {
      "Effect": "Allow",
      "Action": [
        "s3:GetObject",
        "s3:PutObject",
        "s3:DeleteObject",
        "s3:ListBucket"
      ],
      "Resource": [
        "arn:aws:s3:::anihpj-static-files/*",
        "arn:aws:s3:::anihpj-media-uploads/*"
      ]
    },
    {
      "Effect": "Allow",
      "Action": [
        "rds:DescribeDBInstances",
        "rds:Connect"
      ],
      "Resource": "arn:aws:rds:us-east-1:123456789012:db:anihpj-db"
    },
    {
      "Effect": "Allow",
      "Action": [
        "cloudwatch:PutMetricData",
        "logs:CreateLogGroup",
        "logs:CreateLogStream",
        "logs:PutLogEvents"
      ],
      "Resource": "*"
    },
    {
      "Effect": "Allow",
      "Action": [
        "ses:SendEmail",
        "ses:SendRawEmail"
      ],
      "Resource": "*",
      "Condition": {
        "StringEquals": {
          "ses:FromAddress": "noreply@anihpj.com"
        }
      }
    }
  ]
}
# Create role
aws iam create-role \
    --role-name anihpj-ec2-role \
    --assume-role-policy-document file://trust-policy.json

# Attach policy
aws iam put-role-policy \
    --role-name anihpj-ec2-role \
    --policy-name anihpj-permissions \
    --policy-document file://permissions.json

# Create instance profile
aws iam create-instance-profile \
    --instance-profile-name anihpj-ec2-profile

# Add role to profile
aws iam add-role-to-instance-profile \
    --instance-profile-name anihpj-ec2-profile \
    --role-name anihpj-ec2-role

# Attach to EC2 instance
aws ec2 associate-iam-instance-profile \
    --instance-id i-0abc123def456789 \
    --iam-instance-profile Name=anihpj-ec2-profile
вң… Security Best Practice: Never store AWS credentials in your Django code! Always use IAM roles for EC2 instances to access other AWS services securely.
рҹ”җ Encryption Options
# Enable EBS encryption by default in your account
aws ec2 enable-ebs-encryption-by-default

# Create encrypted EBS volume
aws ec2 create-volume \
    --volume-type gp3 \
    --size 30 \
    --availability-zone us-east-1a \
    --encrypted \
    --kms-key-id arn:aws:kms:us-east-1:123456789012:key/abcd1234 \
    --tag-specifications 'ResourceType=volume,Tags=[{Key=Name,Value=anihpj-encrypted-data}]'

# Encryption features:
# вң… Data encrypted at rest
# вң… Data encrypted in transit (between EC2 and EBS)
# вң… Snapshots automatically encrypted
# вң… KMS key management for compliance
# вң… No performance impact

# For Django: Encrypt volumes containing:
# вҖў Database files
# вҖў User uploaded data (resumes)
# вҖў Application logs
# вҖў Backup files

рҹҡЁ CloudWatch Alarms for anihpj
# Create CPU alarm
aws cloudwatch put-metric-alarm \
    --alarm-name anihpj-high-cpu \
    --alarm-description "Alert when CPU exceeds 80%" \
    --metric-name CPUUtilization \
    --namespace AWS/EC2 \
    --statistic Average \
    --period 300 \
    --threshold 80 \
    --comparison-operator GreaterThanThreshold \
    --evaluation-periods 2 \
    --dimensions Name=InstanceId,Value=i-0abc123def456789 \
    --alarm-actions arn:aws:sns:us-east-1:123456789012:anihpj-alerts

# Create disk alarm
aws cloudwatch put-metric-alarm \
    --alarm-name anihpj-low-disk-space \
    --alarm-description "Alert when disk usage exceeds 85%" \
    --metric-name disk_used_percent \
    --namespace CWAgent \
    --statistic Average \
    --period 300 \
    --threshold 85 \
    --comparison-operator GreaterThanThreshold \
    --evaluation-periods 1 \
    --dimensions Name=InstanceId,Value=i-0abc123def456789 \
    --alarm-actions arn:aws:sns:us-east-1:123456789012:anihpj-alerts

# Create memory alarm
aws cloudwatch put-metric-alarm \
    --alarm-name anihpj-high-memory \
    --alarm-description "Alert when memory exceeds 90%" \
    --metric-name mem_used_percent \
    --namespace CWAgent \
    --statistic Average \
    --period 300 \
    --threshold 90 \
    --comparison-operator GreaterThanThreshold \
    --evaluation-periods 2 \
    --dimensions Name=InstanceId,Value=i-0abc123def456789 \
    --alarm-actions arn:aws:sns:us-east-1:123456789012:anihpj-alerts

# Create status check alarm
aws cloudwatch put-metric-alarm \
    --alarm-name anihpj-instance-status-check \
    --alarm-description "Alert when instance status check fails" \
    --metric-name StatusCheckFailed_Instance \
    --namespace AWS/EC2 \
    --statistic Maximum \
    --period 60 \
    --threshold 0 \
    --comparison-operator GreaterThanThreshold \
    --evaluation-periods 2 \
    --dimensions Name=InstanceId,Value=i-0abc123def456789 \
    --alarm-actions arn:aws:sns:us-east-1:123456789012:anihpj-critical-alerts \
    --treat-missing-data notBreaching
рҹ“қ Custom Django Application Metrics
# anihpj/middleware/cloudwatch_metrics.py
import boto3
from django.utils.deprecation import MiddlewareMixin
from datetime import datetime

class CloudWatchMetricsMiddleware(MiddlewareMixin):
    """Send custom Django metrics to CloudWatch"""
    
    def __init__(self, get_response):
        super().__init__(get_response)
        self.cloudwatch = boto3.client('cloudwatch', region_name='us-east-1')
    
    def process_response(self, request, response):
        # Track response times
        if hasattr(request, '_start_time'):
            response_time = (datetime.now() - request._start_time).total_seconds()
            
            self.cloudwatch.put_metric_data(
                Namespace='AnihpjJobPortal',
                MetricData=[
                    {
                        'MetricName': 'ResponseTime',
                        'Value': response_time,
                        'Unit': 'Seconds',
                        'Dimensions': [
                            {'Name': 'View', 'Value': request.path},
                            {'Name': 'Method', 'Value': request.method}
                        ]
                    }
                ]
            )
        
        # Track HTTP status codes
        self.cloudwatch.put_metric_data(
            Namespace='AnihpjJobPortal',
            MetricData=[
                {
                    'MetricName': 'HTTPStatusCode',
                    'Value': 1,
                    'Unit': 'Count',
                    'Dimensions': [
                        {'Name': 'StatusCode', 'Value': str(response.status_code)},
                        {'Name': 'Path', 'Value': request.path}
                    ]
                }
            ]
        )
        
        return response
    
    def process_request(self, request):
        request._start_time = datetime.now()


# Track custom business metrics
def track_job_post_created(job_post):
    """Track when new job is posted"""
    cloudwatch = boto3.client('cloudwatch')
    cloudwatch.put_metric_data(
        Namespace='AnihpjJobPortal',
        MetricData=[
            {
                'MetricName': 'JobPostsCreated',
                'Value': 1,
                'Unit': 'Count',
                'Dimensions': [
                    {'Name': 'Company', 'Value': job_post.author.company},
                    {'Name': 'JobType', 'Value': job_post.type}
                ]
            }
        ]
    )

def track_job_application(job_post):
    """Track when someone applies to a job"""
    cloudwatch = boto3.client('cloudwatch')
    cloudwatch.put_metric_data(
        Namespace='AnihpjJobPortal',
        MetricData=[
            {
                'MetricName': 'JobApplications',
                'Value': 1,
                'Unit': 'Count',
                'Dimensions': [
                    {'Name': 'JobTitle', 'Value': job_post.title},
                    {'Name': 'Location', 'Value': job_post.location.city}
                ]
            }
        ]
    )

рҹ’° Pricing & Cost Optimization

в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ

в”Ӯ                                                                      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  2. RESERVED INSTANCES (1-3 year commitment, up to 72% savings)     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  m5.large Reserved Instance Pricing:                           в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ                                                                 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ

в”Ӯ  3. SAVINGS PLANS (Flexible commitment, up to 72% savings)          в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ

в”Ӯ  4. SPOT INSTANCES (Unused capacity, up to 90% savings)             в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  m5.large Spot: $0.0288/hour (70% cheaper!)                   в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ                                                                 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  How it works:                                                 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  1. Set max price you're willing to pay                       в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  2. Get instance when spot price < max price                  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  3. AWS can terminate with 2-minute warning                   в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ                                                                 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… Massive savings (50-90%)                                    в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… Good for flexible, fault-tolerant workloads                 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вқҢ Can be interrupted                                          в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вқҢ Not recommended for production web servers                  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ                                                                 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ

в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Batch processing (email notifications)                     в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Data analysis (job market trends)                          в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Testing/staging environments                               в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Background job workers                                     в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ

в”Ӯ  5. DEDICATED HOSTS (Physical server for compliance)                в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ

в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  (Can run multiple instances on same physical server)          в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ                                                                 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… Compliance requirements (bring-your-own-license)            в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… Visibility into sockets, cores, host ID                     в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вқҢ Most expensive option                                       в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Use for: Enterprise compliance needs only                     в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ

в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

RECOMMENDATION FOR ANIHPJ:
в”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғв”Ғ
Development:     t3.micro On-Demand      вҶ’  $7.59/month
Staging:         t3.small On-Demand      вҶ’  $15.18/month  
Production:      m5.large Reserved (1yr) вҶ’  $43.22/month (save $27)
Background Jobs: m5.large Spot           вҶ’  $21.02/month (save $49)

Total Monthly: ~$87/month vs $133 On-Demand (35% savings!)
рҹ’Ў Cost Optimization Strategies for anihpj
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ            COST OPTIMIZATION CHECKLIST                           в”Ӯ
в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  1. Right-Sizing                                                в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Monitor CPU, memory, network usage for 2+ weeks              в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Use AWS Compute Optimizer recommendations                    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Start small (t3.micro) and scale up as needed                в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Review monthly and adjust instance types                     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  Example: anihpj running at 20% CPU on m5.large                 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҶ’ Downgrade to t3.medium                                       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҶ’ Save $39.71/month (56% reduction!)                           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  2. Stop Non-Production Instances                               в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Stop dev/test instances nights & weekends                    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Use scheduled actions (Lambda + EventBridge)                 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Tag instances: AutoStop=true                                 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  Example: Stop dev instance 16 hours/day + weekends             в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҶ’ Running only 8 hrs/day Г— 5 days = 40 hrs/week                в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҶ’ vs 168 hrs/week = Save 76%!                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҶ’ t3.micro: $7.59/month вҶ’ $1.82/month                          в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  3. Use Reserved Instances for Production                       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ 1-year commitment for stable production workloads             в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Mix of 1-year and 3-year for predictable savings             в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Start with No Upfront if cash-constrained                    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  4. Leverage Spot Instances                                     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Use for batch jobs (sending job alert emails)                в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Use for CI/CD pipelines                                      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Use for data processing (analytics)                          в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Set max price to avoid surprises                             в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  5. Optimize Storage                                            в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Use gp3 instead of gp2 (20% cheaper)                          в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Delete old EBS snapshots (automate with lifecycle)           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Move static files to S3 ($0.023/GB vs $0.10/GB for EBS)     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Use S3 Intelligent-Tiering for uploads                       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  Example: 100 GB of static files                                в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҶ’ EBS gp3: $8/month                                            в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҶ’ S3 Standard: $2.30/month                                     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҶ’ Save $5.70/month (71% reduction!)                            в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  6. Use Auto Scaling                                            в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Scale down during low traffic periods                        в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Scale up during peak hours                                   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Min: 1 instance, Max: 4 instances                            в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  Example: Auto scale anihpj                                     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҶ’ 1 instance off-peak (20 hrs/day)                             в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҶ’ 3 instances peak (4 hrs/day)                                 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҶ’ Average: 1.33 instances vs 3 always-on                       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҶ’ Save 55% on compute costs!                                   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  7. Implement Caching                                           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Use ElastiCache (Redis) for sessions                         в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Cache database queries                                       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Use CloudFront CDN for static assets                         в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Reduce EC2 instance size needs                               в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  8. Monitor and Alert                                           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Set up AWS Budgets ($50/month alert)                         в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Enable Cost Anomaly Detection                                в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Review Cost Explorer monthly                                 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Tag all resources for cost allocation                        в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  9. Use Cost Allocation Tags                                    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Tag: Environment=production/staging/dev                      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Tag: Project=anihpj                                          в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Tag: Team=engineering                                        в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Tag: CostCenter=product-development                          в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  10. Optimize Data Transfer                                     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Use VPC endpoints for S3 (no data transfer charges)          в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Keep data in same region                                     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҳ‘ Use CloudFront for international users                       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ

в”Ӯ  Scaling Triggers:                                              в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  рҹ“Ҳ SCALE OUT (Add instances)                               в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў CPU > 70% for 5 minutes  вҶ’ Add 1 instance               в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Memory > 80% for 5 min   вҶ’ Add 1 instance               в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Active connections > 1000 вҶ’ Add 1 instance               в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Scheduled: 8am weekdays  вҶ’ Add 2 instances               в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ                                                             в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  рҹ“ү SCALE IN (Remove instances)                             в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў CPU < 30% for 10 minutes вҶ’ Remove 1 instance            в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў After business hours     вҶ’ Remove 2 instances           в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҖў Weekends (low traffic)   вҶ’ Scale to minimum             в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  Benefits:                                                       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вң… Handle traffic spikes automatically                          в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вң… Reduce costs during low-traffic periods                      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вң… Maintain performance and availability                        в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вң… No manual intervention needed                                в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ

рҹҡҖ Create Launch Template
# Create launch template for anihpj
aws ec2 create-launch-template \
    --launch-template-name anihpj-launch-template \
    --launch-template-data '{
        "ImageId": "ami-0c7217cdde317cfec",
        "InstanceType": "m5.large",
        "KeyName": "anihpj-keypair",
        "IamInstanceProfile": {
            "Name": "anihpj-ec2-profile"
        },
        "SecurityGroupIds": ["sg-0abc123def456789"],
        "UserData": "'$(base64 -w 0 user-data.sh)'",
        "BlockDeviceMappings": [
            {
                "DeviceName": "/dev/sda1",
                "Ebs": {
                    "VolumeSize": 20,
                    "VolumeType": "gp3",
                    "DeleteOnTermination": true,
                    "Encrypted": true
                }
            }
        ],
        "TagSpecifications": [
            {
                "ResourceType": "instance",
                "Tags": [
                    {"Key": "Name", "Value": "anihpj-auto-scaled"},
                    {"Key": "Project", "Value": "anihpj"},
                    {"Key": "Environment", "Value": "production"},
                    {"Key": "ManagedBy", "Value": "AutoScaling"}
                ]
            }
        ],
        "Monitoring": {
            "Enabled": true
        }
    }'
вҡҷпёҸ Create Auto Scaling Group
# Create Auto Scaling Group
aws autoscaling create-auto-scaling-group \
    --auto-scaling-group-name anihpj-asg \
    --launch-template LaunchTemplateName=anihpj-launch-template,Version='$Latest' \
    --min-size 1 \
    --max-size 6 \
    --desired-capacity 2 \
    --default-cooldown 300 \
    --health-check-type ELB \
    --health-check-grace-period 300 \
    --vpc-zone-identifier "subnet-0abc123,subnet-0def456,subnet-0ghi789" \
    --target-group-arns "arn:aws:elasticloadbalancing:us-east-1:123456789012:targetgroup/anihpj-tg/abc123" \
    --tags "Key=Name,Value=anihpj-asg-instance,PropagateAtLaunch=true" \
           "Key=Environment,Value=production,PropagateAtLaunch=true"

# Create scaling policies

# 1. Target Tracking Scaling (Recommended - Simple!)
aws autoscaling put-scaling-policy \
    --auto-scaling-group-name anihpj-asg \
    --policy-name anihpj-target-tracking-cpu \
    --policy-type TargetTrackingScaling \
    --target-tracking-configuration '{
        "PredefinedMetricSpecification": {
            "PredefinedMetricType": "ASGAverageCPUUtilization"
        },
        "TargetValue": 70.0
    }'

# 2. Step Scaling Policy (More control)
aws autoscaling put-scaling-policy \
    --auto-scaling-group-name anihpj-asg \
    --policy-name anihpj-scale-out-policy \
    --policy-type StepScaling \
    --adjustment-type ChangeInCapacity \
    --metric-aggregation-type Average \
    --step-adjustments \
        MetricIntervalLowerBound=0,MetricIntervalUpperBound=10,ScalingAdjustment=1 \
        MetricIntervalLowerBound=10,ScalingAdjustment=2

# 3. Scheduled Scaling (Predictable patterns)
# Scale up weekday mornings
aws autoscaling put-scheduled-update-group-action \
    --auto-scaling-group-name anihpj-asg \
    --scheduled-action-name anihpj-scale-up-morning \
    --recurrence "0 8 * * MON-FRI" \
    --desired-capacity 4

# Scale down weekday evenings
aws autoscaling put-scheduled-update-group-action \
    --auto-scaling-group-name anihpj-asg \
    --scheduled-action-name anihpj-scale-down-evening \
    --recurrence "0 18 * * MON-FRI" \
    --desired-capacity 2

# Scale to minimum on weekends
aws autoscaling put-scheduled-update-group-action \
    --auto-scaling-group-name anihpj-asg \
    --scheduled-action-name anihpj-weekend-minimum \
    --recurrence "0 0 * * SAT" \
    --desired-capacity 1
вҡ–пёҸ Load Balancing
рҹ“Ҡ Load Balancer Types Comparison
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ               ELASTIC LOAD BALANCER TYPES                        в”Ӯ
в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  1. APPLICATION LOAD BALANCER (ALB) - Layer 7 (HTTP/HTTPS)      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… Best for: Django web applications (anihpj)              в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… Path-based routing: /api/* вҶ’ API servers                в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… Host-based routing: api.anihpj.com vs www.anihpj.com    в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… SSL/TLS termination                                      в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… WebSocket support                                        в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… HTTP/2 support                                           в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… Authentication (OIDC, Cognito)                           в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… Request/response headers modification                    в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… Lambda targets support                                   в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ                                                              в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Price: $0.0225/hour + $0.008/LCU-hour                     в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ        (~$16.20/month + data processed)                     в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ                                                              в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Use Case: anihpj Django application вҶҗ RECOMMENDED          в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  2. NETWORK LOAD BALANCER (NLB) - Layer 4 (TCP/UDP)             в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… Ultra-low latency (microseconds)                         в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… Millions of requests per second                          в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… Static IP support                                        в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вң… TCP, UDP, TLS protocols                                  в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вқҢ No path-based routing                                    в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вқҢ No HTTP header inspection                                в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ                                                              в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Use Case: Real-time gaming, IoT, high-performance apps    в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  3. CLASSIC LOAD BALANCER (CLB) - Legacy                        в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  вҡ пёҸ Legacy, use ALB or NLB instead                           в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Layer 4 & 7, but fewer features                           в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Being phased out                                           в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  4. GATEWAY LOAD BALANCER (GWLB) - Layer 3                      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  For virtual appliances (firewalls, IDS/IPS)               в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Not typically used for web applications                   в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
рҹ”§ Configure Application Load Balancer
# 1. Create Target Group
aws elbv2 create-target-group \
    --name anihpj-target-group \
    --protocol HTTP \
    --port 80 \
    --vpc-id vpc-0abc123 \
    --health-check-enabled \
    --health-check-path /health/ \
    --health-check-interval-seconds 30 \
    --health-check-timeout-seconds 5 \
    --healthy-threshold-count 2 \
    --unhealthy-threshold-count 3 \
    --matcher HttpCode=200

# 2. Create Application Load Balancer
aws elbv2 create-load-balancer \
    --name anihpj-alb \
    --subnets subnet-0abc123 subnet-0def456 subnet-0ghi789 \
    --security-groups sg-0alb123 \
    --scheme internet-facing \
    --type application \
    --ip-address-type ipv4 \
    --tags Key=Name,Value=anihpj-alb Key=Environment,Value=production

# Output will include: LoadBalancerArn and DNSName
# DNSName: anihpj-alb-1234567890.us-east-1.elb.amazonaws.com

# 3. Create HTTP Listener (redirect to HTTPS)
aws elbv2 create-listener \
    --load-balancer-arn arn:aws:elasticloadbalancing:us-east-1:123456789012:loadbalancer/app/anihpj-alb/abc123 \
    --protocol HTTP \
    --port 80 \
    --default-actions Type=redirect,RedirectConfig='{Protocol=HTTPS,Port=443,StatusCode=HTTP_301}'

# 4. Create HTTPS Listener
aws elbv2 create-listener \
    --load-balancer-arn arn:aws:elasticloadbalancing:us-east-1:123456789012:loadbalancer/app/anihpj-alb/abc123 \
    --protocol HTTPS \
    --port 443 \
    --certificates CertificateArn=arn:aws:acm:us-east-1:123456789012:certificate/abc123 \
    --ssl-policy ELBSecurityPolicy-TLS-1-2-2017-01 \
    --default-actions Type=forward,TargetGroupArn=arn:aws:elasticloadbalancing:us-east-1:123456789012:targetgroup/anihpj-tg/abc123

# 5. Create path-based routing rules (advanced)
# Route /api/* to API servers
aws elbv2 create-rule \
    --listener-arn arn:aws:elasticloadbalancing:us-east-1:123456789012:listener/app/anihpj-alb/abc123/def456 \
    --priority 10 \
    --conditions Field=path-pattern,Values='/api/*' \
    --actions Type=forward,TargetGroupArn=arn:aws:elasticloadbalancing:us-east-1:123456789012:targetgroup/anihpj-api-tg/xyz789

# Route /static/* to static file servers or S3
aws elbv2 create-rule \
    --listener-arn arn:aws:elasticloadbalancing:us-east-1:123456789012:listener/app/anihpj-alb/abc123/def456 \
    --priority 20 \
    --conditions Field=path-pattern,Values='/static/*' \
    --actions Type=redirect,RedirectConfig='{Protocol=HTTPS,Host=static.anihpj.com,StatusCode=HTTP_301}'
рҹҸҘ Django Health Check Endpoint
# anihpj/jobpost/views.py
from django.http import JsonResponse
from django.db import connection
from django.core.cache import cache
import logging

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

def health_check(request):
    """
    Health check endpoint for ALB
    Returns 200 if healthy, 503 if unhealthy
    """
    health_status = {
        'status': 'healthy',
        'checks': {}
    }
    is_healthy = True
    
    # Check database connectivity
    try:
        with connection.cursor() as cursor:
            cursor.execute("SELECT 1")
            health_status['checks']['database'] = 'ok'
    except Exception as e:
        health_status['checks']['database'] = f'error: {str(e)}'
        is_healthy = False
        logger.error(f"Database health check failed: {e}")
    
    # Check cache connectivity
    try:
        cache.set('health_check', 'ok', 10)
        if cache.get('health_check') == 'ok':
            health_status['checks']['cache'] = 'ok'
        else:
            health_status['checks']['cache'] = 'error'
            is_healthy = False
    except Exception as e:
        health_status['checks']['cache'] = f'error: {str(e)}'
        is_healthy = False
        logger.error(f"Cache health check failed: {e}")
    
    # Check disk space
    import shutil
    try:
        stat = shutil.disk_usage('/')
        free_percent = (stat.free / stat.total) * 100
        if free_percent < 10:
            health_status['checks']['disk'] = f'warning: {free_percent:.1f}% free'
            is_healthy = False
        else:
            health_status['checks']['disk'] = f'ok: {free_percent:.1f}% free'
    except Exception as e:
        health_status['checks']['disk'] = f'error: {str(e)}'
        is_healthy = False
    
    if is_healthy:
        return JsonResponse(health_status, status=200)
    else:
        health_status['status'] = 'unhealthy'
        return JsonResponse(health_status, status=503)

# anihpj/urls.py
from django.urls import path
from jobpost.views import health_check

urlpatterns = [
    # ... other patterns ...
    path('health/', health_check, name='health_check'),
]

рҹ’Ў HA Best Practices for anihpj:
  • Deploy across at least 2 Availability Zones
  • Use Multi-AZ RDS for database
  • Store session data in ElastiCache, not local disk
  • Use S3 for static files and user uploads
  • Implement health checks on all services
  • Set up automated backups and disaster recovery

рҹҺ“ Advanced Topics

рҹҡҖ EC2 Fleet

Launch and manage thousands of EC2 instances with a single request. Mix On-Demand, Reserved, and Spot instances.

# Create EC2 Fleet for anihpj batch processing
aws ec2 create-fleet \
    --launch-template-configs '[
        {
            "LaunchTemplateSpecification": {
                "LaunchTemplateId": "lt-0abc123",
                "Version": "$Latest"
            },
            "Overrides": [
                {"InstanceType": "m5.large", "SubnetId": "subnet-0abc123"},
                {"InstanceType": "m5.xlarge", "SubnetId": "subnet-0def456"}
            ]
        }
    ]' \
    --target-capacity-specification '{
        "TotalTargetCapacity": 10,
        "OnDemandTargetCapacity": 2,
        "SpotTargetCapacity": 8,
        "DefaultTargetCapacityType": "spot"
    }' \
    --spot-options '{
        "AllocationStrategy": "diversified",
        "InstanceInterruptionBehavior": "terminate"
    }'
вҡЎ Enhanced Networking & Placement
рҹ”Ң Elastic Fabric Adapter (EFA) for HPC
EFA provides lower latency and higher throughput than TCP transport
for inter-instance communication.

Use cases:
вҖў Machine learning training (distributed)
вҖў Computational fluid dynamics
вҖў Weather modeling
вҖў Financial simulations

Not needed for typical Django web applications like anihpj.
рҹҺ® GPU Instances for ML Workloads
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ              GPU INSTANCE TYPES FOR ML/AI                        в”Ӯ
в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө

в”Ӯ  вҖў p4d.24xlarge: 8Г— A100 GPUs, $32.77/hour                      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҖў Use for: Large language models, deep learning training       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ

в”Ӯ  вҖў Use for: ML inference, video transcoding                     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  For anihpj Job Portal:                                         в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  If implementing resume parsing with ML or job matching:        в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҖў Use g4dn.xlarge for inference                                в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  вҖў Use Spot instances for training (save 70%)                   в”Ӯ
